* [19 May 2019](https://web.archive.org/web/20200319222423/https://twitter.com/jake_neidert/status/1130206273499226112): Abortion is worse than rape because while rape is a horrible and indefensible crime, the victim is left with their life. Abortion is the murder of the victim, who is left with no life.
